<HEAD>
     <TITLE></TITLE>
</HEAD>
<BODY STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

<P STYLE="margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0; text-align: right"><B>Exhibit 99.1</B></P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 14pt; color: Black"><B>Zion
Oil &amp; Gas Launches Simplified New Stock Unit Option Program</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">Dallas, Texas and Caesarea, Israel &ndash;
November 1, 2016 &ndash; Zion Oil &amp; Gas, Inc. (NASDAQ GM: <B>ZN</B>) announces its new Unit Option program under its Dividend
Reinvestment and Common Stock Purchase Plan (DSPP).</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&ldquo;We are excited to launch this
new Unit Option Program, which if successful, will enable us to begin drilling our long anticipated Megiddo-Jezreel #1 well,&rdquo;
says Victor G. Carrillo, Zion&rsquo;s CEO. &ldquo;This simple and streamlined process enables potential investors to quickly and
easily play a part in Zion&rsquo;s mission for Israel&rsquo;s energy independence.&rdquo;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">Zion Oil &amp; Gas described how past
investors expressed how simple it can be to purchase stock on their website. &ldquo;Very easy,&rdquo; expressed Heather, an investor
from Elmira Heights, New York. &ldquo;So grateful for another opportunity to invest in Israel&rsquo;s future.&rdquo;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in; color: #535353"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; color: #535353"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">An investor from Birmingham,
Alabama, said, &ldquo;It was a very simple process. I completed it on my smart phone.&rdquo;&nbsp; <FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; line-height: 115%">Just
this week, a commentor said, &ldquo;Love the easy-invest website you make available for those who wish to contribute. I also would
like to praise your team at the Dallas location. Every time I call for a question or two... or three, they've been so helpful
in so many ways.&rdquo;</FONT></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in; color: #535353"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; color: #535353"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">Zion has seen how similar
programs over the last few years have brought in thousands of new investors without them having to use a broker or other online
financial institution.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in; color: #535353"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; color: #535353"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&ldquo;We are excited
to offer this Stock Option Unit Program to those investors who believe in supporting Israel and the vision of Zion Oil &amp; Gas.
We believe that Zion&rsquo;s ability to offer investment opportunities, such as this Unit Option program, in ways that appeal
to our investment community helps investors who are excited about participating in our project,&rdquo; said Martin M. van Brauman,
Zion&rsquo;s Senior Vice President and Corporate Treasurer.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">Starting
today, November 1, 2016, and ending January 31, 2017 (unless extended at the company&rsquo;s sole discretion), Zion is
offering this new Unit Option to purchase Units of our securities where each Unit (priced at $10.00) is comprised of seven
(7) shares of Common Stock and seven (7) Common Stock purchase warrants. Each warrant (symbol &ldquo;ZNWAE&rdquo;) affords
participants the opportunity to purchase one share of Common Stock at a warrant exercise price of $1.00.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">The warrants will first become exercisable
on March 3, 2017, the 31<SUP>st</SUP> day following the Unit Option Termination Date (unless extended), and continue to be exercisable
through March 3, 2020 (3 years) at a per share exercise price of $1.00.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">If the Company&rsquo;s Common Stock
closing price trades above $5.00 per share for 15 consecutive trading days at any time prior to the warrant expiration date, Zion
may provide a notice to warrant holders of an early warrant termination within 60 days of the notice. The Unit is priced at $10.00
per Unit and no change will be made to the warrant exercise price of $1.00 per share.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">Zion is dedicated to exploring for oil
and gas onshore Israel and is 100% focused on its Megiddo-Jezreel License, a large area south and west of the Sea of Galilee that
includes the Jezreel and Megiddo valleys. This license gives Zion the exclusive right to explore in an area of approximately 99,000
acres that appears to possess the key geologic ingredients of an active petroleum system with significant exploration potential.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 1 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 2px solid"></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="page-break-before: always; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt">&nbsp;</DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black"></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">Zion plans to begin drill site construction
in November which should take approximately 45-60 days to complete.&nbsp; Upon drill site completion, Zion intends to mobilize
the rig to the location to begin rig-up and acceptance testing. They plan to start drilling their next deep exploratory well,
the Megiddo-Jezreel #1, as soon as possible thereafter, assuming sufficient capital is raised.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><IMG SRC="image_001.jpg" ALT="" STYLE="height: 430px; width: 576px"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="color: #000000"><I>October 24,
2016 - Drilling of 3 shallow boreholes at the pad</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="color: #000000">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="color: #000000">Zion Oil
&amp; Gas, Inc. has filed with the SEC a registration statement (including a prospectus) for the unit program under the DSPP to
which this communication relates. That prospectus and other documents the Company has filed with the SEC may be obtained at no
charge (free) by visiting EDGAR on the SEC website at&nbsp;<U>www.sec.gov</U>. Alternatively, the Company will send you the prospectus
upon request by calling toll free 888-891-9466. Direct links to the SEC location, or to the documents in PDF, may be found on
Zion&rsquo;s home page at&nbsp;<U>www.zionoil.com</U>.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-right: 0; margin-left: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: #000000">Contact:</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: #000000">Zion Oil &amp; Gas, Inc.</FONT></P>
